         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/israelis-retaliate-against-palestinian-minister-for-icc-move-12219f08-0e46-47e9-930d-9fd7da22ef96.html" data-vars-content-id="12219f08-0e46-47e9-930d-9fd7da22ef96" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Israelis retaliate against Palestinian minister for ICC move" data-vars-index="4" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="Israelis retaliate against Palestinian minister for ICC move" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/israelis-retaliate-against-palestinian-minister-for-icc-move-12219f08-0e46-47e9-930d-9fd7da22ef96.html">
          Israelis retaliate against Palestinian minister for ICC move
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/israelis-retaliate-against-palestinian-minister-for-icc-move-12219f08-0e46-47e9-930d-9fd7da22ef96.html" data-vars-content-id="12219f08-0e46-47e9-930d-9fd7da22ef96" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Israelis retaliate against Palestinian minister for ICC move" data-vars-index="4" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="Israelis retaliate against Palestinian minister for ICC move" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/israelis-retaliate-against-palestinian-minister-for-icc-move-12219f08-0e46-47e9-930d-9fd7da22ef96.html" title="Israelis retaliate against Palestinian minister for ICC move">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
           <amp-img alt="Israelis retaliate against Palestinian minister for ICC move" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-format="default" data-testid="amp-tag" height="1080" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/HWxNhbqkW8RL_MGl6zDwB17utb4=/0x51:4097x2356/1920x1080/2021/03/21/1616344958000.jpg" srcset="https://images.axios.com/HWxNhbqkW8RL_MGl6zDwB17utb4=/0x51:4097x2356/1920x1080/2021/03/21/1616344958000.jpg 1920w,https://images.axios.com/in-N4sXxfON-59mOSH2-BPb9vng=/0x51:4097x2356/1600x900/2021/03/21/1616344958000.jpg 1600w,https://images.axios.com/zhGztxmTtJO1tduRs8yDuUsCbWo=/0x51:4097x2356/1366x768/2021/03/21/1616344958000.jpg 1366w,https://images.axios.com/iOvj2p9tQDPq1r8jQ_HECfhZ76A=/0x51:4097x2356/1024x576/2021/03/21/1616344958000.jpg 1024w,https://images.axios.com/1_q_alS0Vmk4PNjN5YYw0lXO_Go=/0x51:4097x2356/768x432/2021/03/21/1616344958000.jpg 768w,https://images.axios.com/oFmvpPK-z8yidiO9LzGE0wyTzhs=/0x51:4097x2356/640x360/2021/03/21/1616344958000.jpg 640w,https://images.axios.com/6xwtStBs-1cWr6mLUKGuCEDWU5c=/0x51:4097x2356/320x180/2021/03/21/1616344958000.jpg 320w" width="1920">
            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>
           </amp-img>
          </div>
         </a>
         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           Palestinian Foreign Minister Riyad al-Maliki. Photo: Reuters/Hannibal Hanschke/Pool/Anadolu Agency via Getty Images
          </p>
         </figcaption>
        </figure>
        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          The Israeli domestic security service Shin Bet revoked Palestinian Foreign Minister Riyad al-Maliki's VIP status when he returned to the West Bank from Jordan today, Axios has learned from Israeli officials.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          According to the officials, the unusual act was retaliation for al-Maliki's push for an investigation against Israel in the International Criminal Court. The card allows easier movement and access inside the West Bank and at border crossings.
         </p>
        </div>

      <h5 class="sc-31t5q3-4 sc-5z731v-0 fDzkOP hidden lg:block text-soft-black-shade">
       1 ✊🏿 thing
      </h5>
      <div class="py-12 sm:py-20 lg:py-0 lg:mb-40 flex border-0 border-b lg:border-none border-accent-blue-tint border-solid">

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/defense-secretary-surprise-afghanistan-0ce9c20c-c1c1-4df5-a29b-c993048211c3.html" data-vars-content-id="0ce9c20c-c1c1-4df5-a29b-c993048211c3" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Defense Secretary Lloyd Austin makes surprise visit to Afghanistan" data-vars-index="5" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="Defense Secretary Lloyd Austin makes surprise visit to Afghanistan" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/defense-secretary-surprise-afghanistan-0ce9c20c-c1c1-4df5-a29b-c993048211c3.html">
          Defense Secretary Lloyd Austin makes surprise visit to Afghanistan
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/defense-secretary-surprise-afghanistan-0ce9c20c-c1c1-4df5-a29b-c993048211c3.html" data-vars-content-id="0ce9c20c-c1c1-4df5-a29b-c993048211c3" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Defense Secretary Lloyd Austin makes surprise visit to Afghanistan" data-vars-index="5" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="Defense Secretary Lloyd Austin makes surprise visit to Afghanistan" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/defense-secretary-surprise-afghanistan-0ce9c20c-c1c1-4df5-a29b-c993048211c3.html" title="Defense Secretary Lloyd Austin makes surprise visit to Afghanistan">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
           <amp-img alt="Defense Secretary Lloyd Austin makes surprise visit to Afghanistan" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-format="default" data-testid="amp-tag" height="1080" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/EwoBThuK-nx-cawqShK050PRDxg=/0x65:4673x2694/1920x1080/2021/03/21/1616340599233.jpg" srcset="https://images.axios.com/EwoBThuK-nx-cawqShK050PRDxg=/0x65:4673x2694/1920x1080/2021/03/21/1616340599233.jpg 1920w,https://images.axios.com/ujdhXgGjanQYpTyoNGAV6pZ7Amc=/0x65:4673x2694/1600x900/2021/03/21/1616340599233.jpg 1600w,https://images.axios.com/0ehdBGIZMkljMhFgeNnTaP9yFOc=/0x65:4673x2694/1366x768/2021/03/21/1616340599233.jpg 1366w,https://images.axios.com/bYRZ4xrCxL01BHEThQnHGEjTZbE=/0x65:4673x2694/1024x576/2021/03/21/1616340599233.jpg 1024w,https://images.axios.com/XE-zxPdhysYP18LfjoDfCYFNsXY=/0x65:4673x2694/768x432/2021/03/21/1616340599233.jpg 768w,https://images.axios.com/xchYiujE4W6hXnZ6Z6vWX2NZlyg=/0x65:4673x2694/640x360/2021/03/21/1616340599233.jpg 640w,https://images.axios.com/RalIN7YXyCnl5Lswi2fiVTJ86cg=/0x65:4673x2694/320x180/2021/03/21/1616340599233.jpg 320w" width="1920">
            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>
           </amp-img>

         </a>
         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           Defense Secretary Lloyd Austin. Photo:
           <strong>
           </strong>
           Tom Williams/CQ-Roll Call, Inc via Getty Images
          </p>
         </figcaption>

        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          U.S. Defense Secretary Lloyd Austin traveled to Afghanistan on Sunday for a previously unannounced visit, where he met with Afghan President Ashraf Ghani in Kabul,
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.politico.com/news/2021/03/21/pentagon-austin-afghanistan-surprise-stop-477375" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="3" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="Politico" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.politico.com/news/2021/03/21/pentagon-austin-afghanistan-surprise-stop-477375" target="_blank">
           Politico
          </a>
          reports.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          Austin's visit comes as the U.S. continues to debate whether to abide by an agreement, brokered by the Trump administration, to withdraw U.S. troops from Afghanistan by May 1.
         </p>

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/national-holiday-emancipation-e9e8dc33-04e7-4390-a3bb-c1d867b3e036.html" data-vars-content-id="e9e8dc33-04e7-4390-a3bb-c1d867b3e036" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="National holiday eyed to commemorate emancipation" data-vars-index="6" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="National holiday eyed to commemorate emancipation" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/national-holiday-emancipation-e9e8dc33-04e7-4390-a3bb-c1d867b3e036.html">
          National holiday eyed to commemorate emancipation
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/national-holiday-emancipation-e9e8dc33-04e7-4390-a3bb-c1d867b3e036.html" data-vars-content-id="e9e8dc33-04e7-4390-a3bb-c1d867b3e036" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="National holiday eyed to commemorate emancipation" data-vars-index="6" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="National holiday eyed to commemorate emancipation" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/national-holiday-emancipation-e9e8dc33-04e7-4390-a3bb-c1d867b3e036.html" title="National holiday eyed to commemorate emancipation">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
           <amp-img alt="National holiday eyed to commemorate emancipation" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-format="default" data-testid="amp-tag" height="1080" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/-ri1Dk28RROOdoXH-cKUw4cqy7A=/0x0:3000x1688/1920x1080/2021/03/16/1615858709887.jpg" srcset="https://images.axios.com/-ri1Dk28RROOdoXH-cKUw4cqy7A=/0x0:3000x1688/1920x1080/2021/03/16/1615858709887.jpg 1920w,https://images.axios.com/u51Lh18CzlRIg25LunVOYQJQU5I=/0x0:3000x1688/1600x900/2021/03/16/1615858709887.jpg 1600w,https://images.axios.com/uyj98PRVlhA-Zp6DACystwcOpxQ=/0x0:3000x1688/1366x768/2021/03/16/1615858709887.jpg 1366w,https://images.axios.com/cFsWApfHT2SlYgOTeMLmSVkPb_8=/0x0:3000x1688/1024x576/2021/03/16/1615858709887.jpg 1024w,https://images.axios.com/tJBuOXZmDQSWvNyDSaRwGztmIHg=/0x0:3000x1688/768x432/2021/03/16/1615858709887.jpg 768w,https://images.axios.com/DLS98BqtIKROdlHlglXwXP5aTvU=/0x0:3000x1688/640x360/2021/03/16/1615858709887.jpg 640w,https://images.axios.com/V9fiRewWUR3ExqqzYu6MIoHLaVY=/0x0:3000x1688/320x180/2021/03/16/1615858709887.jpg 320w" width="1920">
            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>
           </amp-img>
          </div>
         </a>
         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           A man displays a shirt during a Juneteenth celebration in Tulsa, Okla. Photo: Michael B. Thomas/Getty Images
          </p>
         </figcaption>
        </figure>
        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          A proposal in the Congress would designate June 19 as a national holiday to commemorate the emancipation of enslaved people in the United States. But a key Black congressman says another day might be better.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          The nation is struggling with how to commemorate and discuss emancipation amid a racial awaking, and the disagreement about even the date that it should be marked shows the effort still faces some major obstacles.
         </p>
        </div>

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/tax-season-irs-pandemic-91ae6dde-f63e-49fb-9d55-cf2fe6ad3238.html" data-vars-content-id="91ae6dde-f63e-49fb-9d55-cf2fe6ad3238" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="One of the most complex tax seasons ever" data-vars-index="7" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="One of the most complex tax seasons ever" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/tax-season-irs-pandemic-91ae6dde-f63e-49fb-9d55-cf2fe6ad3238.html">

         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/tax-season-irs-pandemic-91ae6dde-f63e-49fb-9d55-cf2fe6ad3238.html" data-vars-content-id="91ae6dde-f63e-49fb-9d55-cf2fe6ad3238" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="One of the most complex tax seasons ever" data-vars-index="7" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="One of the most complex tax seasons ever" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/tax-season-irs-pandemic-91ae6dde-f63e-49fb-9d55-cf2fe6ad3238.html" title="One of the most complex tax seasons ever">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
           <amp-img alt="One of the most complex tax seasons ever" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-format="default" data-testid="amp-tag" height="1080" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/Z-GoY4epuxiVXX4_ylt8ZtDXwHg=/0x0:1920x1080/1920x1080/2021/03/19/1616177239387.jpg" srcset="https://images.axios.com/Z-GoY4epuxiVXX4_ylt8ZtDXwHg=/0x0:1920x1080/1920x1080/2021/03/19/1616177239387.jpg 1920w,https://images.axios.com/kYpQOTIuFCzUtUQ5CtXtu49vvio=/0x0:1920x1080/1600x900/2021/03/19/1616177239387.jpg 1600w,https://images.axios.com/SVMticuwqHSXT8csdCeYh_9jMS0=/0x0:1920x1080/1366x768/2021/03/19/1616177239387.jpg 1366w,https://images.axios.com/-ZT7JZ5oSgsqfxa1fBY8Yv24jjs=/0x0:1920x1080/1024x576/2021/03/19/1616177239387.jpg 1024w,https://images.axios.com/aNBrNZin6rPEjCUBqkBK4dPH28c=/0x0:1920x1080/768x432/2021/03/19/1616177239387.jpg 768w,https://images.axios.com/0h2s8Y6NLjGJzusJHJ5IwHW1ZG8=/0x0:1920x1080/640x360/2021/03/19/1616177239387.jpg 640w,https://images.axios.com/luESjZVycIJspA04v-dL5d99TnA=/0x0:1920x1080/320x180/2021/03/19/1616177239387.jpg 320w" width="1920">
            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>
           </amp-img>
          </div>
         </a>
         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           Illustration: Sarah Grillo/Axios
          </p>
         </figcaption>
        </figure>
        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          This year's tax season is shaping up to be a gnarly one. The IRS has agreed to give Americans an extra month to file their taxes — but that's barely going to be enough to help them and their accountants when it comes to navigating the new code.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          The U.S. tax filing system is painful and complex — largely by design.
         </p>
        </div>

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-shootings-victims-cherokee-county-fd653c24-c81c-43db-b807-02627b73e6e8.html" data-vars-content-id="fd653c24-c81c-43db-b807-02627b73e6e8" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="What we know about the victims of the Georgia shootings" data-vars-index="9" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="What we know about the victims of the Georgia shootings" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-shootings-victims-cherokee-county-fd653c24-c81c-43db-b807-02627b73e6e8.html">
          What we know about the victims of the Georgia shootings
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-shootings-victims-cherokee-county-fd653c24-c81c-43db-b807-02627b73e6e8.html" data-vars-content-id="fd653c24-c81c-43db-b807-02627b73e6e8" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="What we know about the victims of the Georgia shootings" data-vars-index="9" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="What we know about the victims of the Georgia shootings" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-shootings-victims-cherokee-county-fd653c24-c81c-43db-b807-02627b73e6e8.html" title="What we know about the victims of the Georgia shootings">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">

            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>

         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           Mourners leave flowers for the victims of the Georgia shooting. Photo: Megan Varner/Getty Images
          </p>

        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          The eight people who died in a shooting spree by a 21-year-old gunman in Georgia this week have been identified by police and Fulton County officials.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          The fact that six of the eight victims are Asian women has left Asians and Pacific Islanders across America
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-spa-shooting-asian-american-hate-crimes-232d362d-72bd-49eb-8658-28dca61dfc53.html" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="6" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="fearful and alarmed" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-spa-shooting-asian-american-hate-crimes-232d362d-72bd-49eb-8658-28dca61dfc53.html" target="_self">
           fearful and alarmed
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </div>

          Thousands ordered to evacuate as "one-in-100-year" floods hit Australia
         </a>
        </h3>

         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/australia-floods-thousands-sydney-evacuation-orders-d690de09-730e-45e3-a46f-8d6e38024b03.html" data-vars-content-id="d690de09-730e-45e3-a46f-8d6e38024b03" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline='Thousands ordered to evacuate as "one-in-100-year" floods hit Australia' data-vars-index="10" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text='Thousands ordered to evacuate as "one-in-100-year" floods hit Australia' data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/australia-floods-thousands-sydney-evacuation-orders-d690de09-730e-45e3-a46f-8d6e38024b03.html" title='Thousands ordered to evacuate as "one-in-100-year" floods hit Australia'>

           A rescue worker helps residents cross a flooded road during heavy rain in western Sydney on Saturday. Photo: Saeed Khan/AFP via Getty Images

        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          Australia's east coast is being hit by record rainfall, with flood warnings issued and
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.emergency.nsw.gov.au/Documents/publications/agrn-960-nsw-storms-floods-march-10-onwards-media-release.pdf" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="7" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="a natural disaster" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.emergency.nsw.gov.au/Documents/publications/agrn-960-nsw-storms-floods-march-10-onwards-media-release.pdf" target="_blank">
           a natural disaster
          </a>
          declared for parts of the most populous state, New South Wales (NSW).
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Details:
          </strong>
          NSW premier Gladys Berejiklian
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.facebook.com/gladysnsw/videos/759790834907461/" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="7" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="told a briefing" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.facebook.com/gladysnsw/videos/759790834907461/" target="_blank">
           told a briefing
          </a>
          Sunday western Sydney faced a flooding event not seen for half a century, while parts of the Mid North Coast were facing a "one-in-100-year event."
         </p>

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-rally-against-anti-asian-hate-photos-01607b2e-e105-404b-8eea-4edf30105d15.html" data-vars-content-id="01607b2e-e105-404b-8eea-4edf30105d15" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="In photos: Protesters rally against anti-Asian hate in Atlanta and across U.S." data-vars-index="11" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="In photos: Protesters rally against anti-Asian hate in Atlanta and across U.S." data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-rally-against-anti-asian-hate-photos-01607b2e-e105-404b-8eea-4edf30105d15.html">
          In photos: Protesters rally against anti-Asian hate in Atlanta and across U.S.
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-rally-against-anti-asian-hate-photos-01607b2e-e105-404b-8eea-4edf30105d15.html" data-vars-content-id="01607b2e-e105-404b-8eea-4edf30105d15" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="In photos: Protesters rally against anti-Asian hate in Atlanta and across U.S." data-vars-index="11" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="In photos: Protesters rally against anti-Asian hate in Atlanta and across U.S." data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-rally-against-anti-asian-hate-photos-01607b2e-e105-404b-8eea-4edf30105d15.html" title="In photos: Protesters rally against anti-Asian hate in Atlanta and across U.S.">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
           <amp-img alt="In photos: Protesters rally against anti-Asian hate in Atlanta and across U.S." class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-format="default" data-testid="amp-tag" height="1080" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/uiABl3CdbFis2Nr3luQmqzxafCM=/0x200:6000x3575/1920x1080/2021/03/20/1616282004666.jpg" srcset="https://images.axios.com/uiABl3CdbFis2Nr3luQmqzxafCM=/0x200:6000x3575/1920x1080/2021/03/20/1616282004666.jpg 1920w,https://images.axios.com/oqsL7xUi1BUFb0J96T3l9zipo8I=/0x200:6000x3575/1600x900/2021/03/20/1616282004666.jpg 1600w,https://images.axios.com/xb8KuMfTPNlA--4uyZfcL4GmB2E=/0x200:6000x3575/1366x768/2021/03/20/1616282004666.jpg 1366w,https://images.axios.com/NPNwH0-W3FUMH9NWeZ0Wq6O7wMU=/0x200:6000x3575/1024x576/2021/03/20/1616282004666.jpg 1024w,https://images.axios.com/DhhuIRsW9dpXxJVtHxNB-REjixo=/0x200:6000x3575/768x432/2021/03/20/1616282004666.jpg 768w,https://images.axios.com/4p6Phn8ekRQsEWA_B_1ArO8mC3w=/0x200:6000x3575/640x360/2021/03/20/1616282004666.jpg 640w,https://images.axios.com/BeKS2IwkHh4AcqrE72ySC1Eny1I=/0x200:6000x3575/320x180/2021/03/20/1616282004666.jpg 320w" width="1920">
            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>
           </amp-img>
          </div>
         </a>
         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           Demonstrators take to the streets of Atlanta to show support for Asian and Pacific Islander (AAPI) communities on March 20 in Georgia. Photo: Megan Varner/Getty Images
          </p>
         </figcaption>
        </figure>
        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          Hundreds of protesters gathered in Atlanta, Georgia, Saturday to honor the eight people killed in
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/georgia-massage-parlor-shooting-8-dead-arrest-715fc40a-7e80-444d-82d3-5b39655f0512.html" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="8" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="this week's spa shootings" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.axios.com/georgia-massage-parlor-shooting-8-dead-arrest-715fc40a-7e80-444d-82d3-5b39655f0512.html" target="_self">
           this week's spa shootings
          </a>
          in the city, with many chanting "Stop Asian hate," per the
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.nytimes.com/2021/03/20/us/stopasianhate-protest-atlanta.html" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="8" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="New York Times" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2021/03/20/us/stopasianhate-protest-atlanta.html" target="_blank">
           New York Times
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           The big picture:
          </strong>
          Six women of Asian descent were among those to lose their lives in the shootings. The Atlanta rally was
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://edition.cnn.com/2021/03/20/us/metro-atlanta-shootings-saturday/index.html?utm_content=2021-03-20T22%3A31%3A03&amp;utm_source=twCNN&amp;utm_medium=social&amp;utm_term=link" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="8" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="one of several" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://edition.cnn.com/2021/03/20/us/metro-atlanta-shootings-saturday/index.html?utm_content=2021-03-20T22%3A31%3A03&amp;utm_source=twCNN&amp;utm_medium=social&amp;utm_term=link" target="_blank">
           one of several
          </a>
          being held across the U.S. Saturday to honor those killed in the attack and to denounce a
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/anti-asian-hate-report-89ff12fb-f4ef-4eea-946a-c755e786f043.html" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="8" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="surge in violence" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.axios.com/anti-asian-hate-report-89ff12fb-f4ef-4eea-946a-c755e786f043.html" target="_self">
           surge in violence
          </a>
          and
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/elderly-asian-woman-attack-san-francisco-70924914-c250-48c5-90b6-e7b20ecf2403.html" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="8" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="hate incidents" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.axios.com/elderly-asian-woman-attack-san-francisco-70924914-c250-48c5-90b6-e7b20ecf2403.html" target="_self">
           hate incidents
          </a>
          against Asian Americans.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="sm:flex sm:items-end sm:flex-wrap -mt-12">
         <a class="sc-31t5q3-10 kHAPjX sc-19f8cds-0 iBVeYd whitespace-no-wrap block mt-12 sm:flex-grow gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-rally-against-anti-asian-hate-photos-01607b2e-e105-404b-8eea-4edf30105d15.html" data-vars-content-id="01607b2e-e105-404b-8eea-4edf30105d15" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="In photos: Protesters rally against anti-Asian hate in Atlanta and across U.S." data-vars-index="11" data-vars-item="go_deeper" data-vars-link-text="In photos: Protesters rally against anti-Asian hate in Atlanta and across U.S." data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/atlanta-rally-against-anti-asian-hate-photos-01607b2e-e105-404b-8eea-4edf30105d15.html">

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/julia-letlow-wins-louisiana-house-race-luke-62d3dd45-2105-41f5-b6f8-34b82996c07c.html" data-vars-content-id="62d3dd45-2105-41f5-b6f8-34b82996c07c" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Julia Letlow wins House race in Louisiana to replace her husband" data-vars-index="12" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="Julia Letlow wins House race in Louisiana to replace her husband" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/julia-letlow-wins-louisiana-house-race-luke-62d3dd45-2105-41f5-b6f8-34b82996c07c.html">
          Julia Letlow wins House race in Louisiana to replace her husband
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/julia-letlow-wins-louisiana-house-race-luke-62d3dd45-2105-41f5-b6f8-34b82996c07c.html" data-vars-content-id="62d3dd45-2105-41f5-b6f8-34b82996c07c" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Julia Letlow wins House race in Louisiana to replace her husband" data-vars-index="12" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="Julia Letlow wins House race in Louisiana to replace her husband" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/julia-letlow-wins-louisiana-house-race-luke-62d3dd45-2105-41f5-b6f8-34b82996c07c.html" title="Julia Letlow wins House race in Louisiana to replace her husband">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
           <amp-img alt="Julia Letlow wins House race in Louisiana to replace her husband" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-format="default" data-testid="amp-tag" height="1080" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/AH4j8EW7S3Cpyzr0g9ZpXHDuK7M=/0x0:6000x3375/1920x1080/2021/03/19/1616188562346.None" srcset="https://images.axios.com/AH4j8EW7S3Cpyzr0g9ZpXHDuK7M=/0x0:6000x3375/1920x1080/2021/03/19/1616188562346.None 1920w,https://images.axios.com/PeT0MIkr_yYUroncs4Uo7CV8guI=/0x0:6000x3375/1600x900/2021/03/19/1616188562346.None 1600w,https://images.axios.com/ahlB3bXWLHEQxDE2QlyAipJsg1s=/0x0:6000x3375/1366x768/2021/03/19/1616188562346.None 1366w,https://images.axios.com/pya2hbY3G8v3i9pIPimXscavyPU=/0x0:6000x3375/1024x576/2021/03/19/1616188562346.None 1024w,https://images.axios.com/cQMgopmz6oPAlV90eAN40kML2xY=/0x0:6000x3375/768x432/2021/03/19/1616188562346.None 768w,https://images.axios.com/t2ficgQB99R7N4ryLTVnIHqyxzo=/0x0:6000x3375/640x360/2021/03/19/1616188562346.None 640w,https://images.axios.com/mnec2EHg0nFowiZvuvFQ2apFppk=/0x0:6000x3375/320x180/2021/03/19/1616188562346.None 320w" width="1920">
            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>

         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           Members in January holding a moment of silence for Letlow. Photo: Erin Scott-Pool/Getty Images
          </p>
         </figcaption>

        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          Julia Letlow (R) on Saturday won Louisiana's 5th congressional district's special election for the U.S. House,
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://apnews.com/article/donald-trump-new-orleans-coronavirus-pandemic-elections-house-elections-548aa6d0a30136b580f1d4138bb02f4d" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="9" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="AP reports" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://apnews.com/article/donald-trump-new-orleans-coronavirus-pandemic-elections-house-elections-548aa6d0a30136b580f1d4138bb02f4d" target="_blank">
           AP reports
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          Letlow will now replace her late husband, Rep.-elect Luke Letlow (R), who passed away from COVID-19 in December. He was just 41 years old. She received a resounding endorsement from former President Trump, who said she is "so outstanding."
         </p>

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/miami-beach-curfew-emergency-spring-break-crowds-30428ef2-e7c4-49d4-85d7-26c3d4729173.html" data-vars-content-id="30428ef2-e7c4-49d4-85d7-26c3d4729173" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Miami Beach declares curfew over spring break crowds" data-vars-index="14" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="Miami Beach declares curfew over spring break crowds" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/miami-beach-curfew-emergency-spring-break-crowds-30428ef2-e7c4-49d4-85d7-26c3d4729173.html">
          Miami Beach declares curfew over spring break crowds
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/miami-beach-curfew-emergency-spring-break-crowds-30428ef2-e7c4-49d4-85d7-26c3d4729173.html" data-vars-content-id="30428ef2-e7c4-49d4-85d7-26c3d4729173" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Miami Beach declares curfew over spring break crowds" data-vars-index="14" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="Miami Beach declares curfew over spring break crowds" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/miami-beach-curfew-emergency-spring-break-crowds-30428ef2-e7c4-49d4-85d7-26c3d4729173.html" title="Miami Beach declares curfew over spring break crowds">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
           <amp-img alt="Miami Beach declares curfew over spring break crowds" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-format="default" data-testid="amp-tag" height="1080" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/M5m2CkpeRVg1w5xoIpNoHWH1byk=/0x221:3000x1909/1920x1080/2021/03/20/1616275971772.jpg" srcset="https://images.axios.com/M5m2CkpeRVg1w5xoIpNoHWH1byk=/0x221:3000x1909/1920x1080/2021/03/20/1616275971772.jpg 1920w,https://images.axios.com/NgXFA_1_aQdSGo1PsD2A1bejd3Q=/0x221:3000x1909/1600x900/2021/03/20/1616275971772.jpg 1600w,https://images.axios.com/skqTMEGfpu-Ugn-YVcsB9tM1Pvg=/0x221:3000x1909/1366x768/2021/03/20/1616275971772.jpg 1366w,https://images.axios.com/4qTNrfMFa7DQ6fRJBqDrO5RHycA=/0x221:3000x1909/1024x576/2021/03/20/1616275971772.jpg 1024w,https://images.axios.com/L_eaWdACE5GzTzFui0AA87qvz4I=/0x221:3000x1909/768x432/2021/03/20/1616275971772.jpg 768w,https://images.axios.com/5oMOdUWQte51IEZQR7RkzHqny3I=/0x221:3000x1909/640x360/2021/03/20/1616275971772.jpg 640w,https://images.axios.com/4H5fxNATDvKRpjC8SMipocPaLQQ=/0x221:3000x1909/320x180/2021/03/20/1616275971772.jpg 320w" width="1920">
            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>
           </amp-img>
          </div>
         </a>
         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           People gathered in Miami Beach, Florida, for spring break on March 18. Photo: Joe Raedle/Getty Images
          </p>
         </figcaption>
        </figure>
        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          The city of Miami Beach
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://twitter.com/MiamiBeachNews/status/1373387865992925191?s=20" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="10" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="declared a state of emergency" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://twitter.com/MiamiBeachNews/status/1373387865992925191?s=20" target="_blank">
           declared a state of emergency
          </a>
          and imposed an 8 p.m. curfew for the entertainment district because spring breakers were gathering in crowds around the city despite the coronavirus pandemic.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          Interim City Manager Raul Aguila said the emergency measures will be in effect for at least 72 hours in an effort to prevent widespread COVID-19 transmission. City leaders will meet Monday and vote on whether to extend the order or cancel it.
         </p>
        </div>

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/cbp-5000-unaccompanied-children-9034faf0-1dfc-4b2d-98fb-5f985734014b.html" data-vars-content-id="9034faf0-1dfc-4b2d-98fb-5f985734014b" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="CBP has more than 5,000 unaccompanied children in its custody" data-vars-index="15" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="CBP has more than 5,000 unaccompanied children in its custody" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/cbp-5000-unaccompanied-children-9034faf0-1dfc-4b2d-98fb-5f985734014b.html">
          CBP has more than 5,000 unaccompanied children in its custody
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/cbp-5000-unaccompanied-children-9034faf0-1dfc-4b2d-98fb-5f985734014b.html" data-vars-content-id="9034faf0-1dfc-4b2d-98fb-5f985734014b" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="CBP has more than 5,000 unaccompanied children in its custody" data-vars-index="15" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="CBP has more than 5,000 unaccompanied children in its custody" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/cbp-5000-unaccompanied-children-9034faf0-1dfc-4b2d-98fb-5f985734014b.html" title="CBP has more than 5,000 unaccompanied children in its custody">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
           <amp-img alt="CBP has more than 5,000 unaccompanied children in its custody" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-format="default" data-testid="amp-tag" height="1080" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/FcTV8NOz7se7tVAzCF3VDun3UZw=/0x520:5000x3333/1920x1080/2021/03/20/1616273635526.jpg" srcset="https://images.axios.com/FcTV8NOz7se7tVAzCF3VDun3UZw=/0x520:5000x3333/1920x1080/2021/03/20/1616273635526.jpg 1920w,https://images.axios.com/OU7pMOqRcoA5YQJSCYNEcJxG_Dk=/0x520:5000x3333/1600x900/2021/03/20/1616273635526.jpg 1600w,https://images.axios.com/n8gFHYAf1PxH1mbL0N287N2Bwq0=/0x520:5000x3333/1366x768/2021/03/20/1616273635526.jpg 1366w,https://images.axios.com/11CVzlbTc433467W3tF8Sp1UgPE=/0x520:5000x3333/1024x576/2021/03/20/1616273635526.jpg 1024w,https://images.axios.com/hxI4kXuymTgxh42EUf0BWflm-wY=/0x520:5000x3333/768x432/2021/03/20/1616273635526.jpg 768w,https://images.axios.com/43DB3al6b4zkPVjQtqopz81DpOk=/0x520:5000x3333/640x360/2021/03/20/1616273635526.jpg 640w,https://images.axios.com/9nTLPLXsIAZlOaY45by37NhUjm4=/0x520:5000x3333/320x180/2021/03/20/1616273635526.jpg 320w" width="1920">
            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>
           </amp-img>
          </div>
         </a>
         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           Border Patrol agents apprehending a group of immigrants near El Paso, Texas, on March 15. Photo: Justin Hamel/AFP via Getty Images
          </p>

        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          Customs and Border Protection has more than 5,000 unaccompanied children in its custody, up from
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://twitter.com/StefWKight/status/1372670760871985161?s=20" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="11" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="less than 4,500 just days" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://twitter.com/StefWKight/status/1372670760871985161?s=20" target="_blank">
           less than 4,500 just days
          </a>
          ago, according to agency documents reviewed by
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.cnn.com/2021/03/20/politics/unaccompanied-migrant-children-cbp/index.html?utm_term=link&amp;utm_content=2021-03-20T20%3A34%3A04&amp;utm_medium=social&amp;utm_source=twCNNp" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="11" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="CNN" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.cnn.com/2021/03/20/politics/unaccompanied-migrant-children-cbp/index.html?utm_term=link&amp;utm_content=2021-03-20T20%3A34%3A04&amp;utm_medium=social&amp;utm_source=twCNNp" target="_blank">
           CNN
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          The number of unaccompanied children crossing the border is expected to grow exponentially through this spring, which is likely to further strain the resources needed to shelter the children, setting up a crisis for the Biden administration.
         </p>

        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          Six of the eight victims that an Atlanta area assailant gunned down this Tuesday night were Asian women, but whether those shootings will be prosecuted as hate crimes remains unknown as investigations continue.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          "As the debate over what legally qualifies as anti-Asian bias unfolds, the community is grappling with the reality that the law is simply not designed to account for many of the ways in which Asian-Americans experience racism," the
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.nytimes.com/2021/03/18/nyregion/asian-hate-crimes.html?smid=url-share" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="12" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="New York Times writes" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2021/03/18/nyregion/asian-hate-crimes.html?smid=url-share" target="_blank">
           New York Times writes
          </a>
          .
         </p>

          Fauci: U.K. variant may account for 30% of U.S. coronavirus infections
         </a>

           Anthony Fauci during a Senate hearing committee on March 18. Photo: Anna Moneymaker/The New York Times/Bloomberg via Getty Images

        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          The coronavirus variant first discovered in the United Kingdom may account for up to 30% of new COVID infections across the U.S., NIAID Director Anthony Fauci said during
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://youtu.be/qOIuzWDmHxg?t=999" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="13" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="a White House briefing" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://youtu.be/qOIuzWDmHxg?t=999" target="_blank">
           a White House briefing
          </a>
          on the virus Friday.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          The variant, called B.1.1.7, has been detected throughout the U.S., and studies have suggested it appears to spread more easily than the original strain of the virus.
         </p>

      <div class="sc-1jy24uc-0 ehZYCh full gtm-content-click pt-20 up-to-sm:pt-12" data-testid="au-container">
       <div class="sc-1jy24uc-3 jFfnFy grid-layout">
        <div class="flex items-center caption mb-12">
         <div class="w-20 h-20 mr-6 sc-6usfji-0 lbJFqa">
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/authors/newsdesk/" data-vars-content-id="05318243-dc9d-4334-a041-42403824eafe" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Hard Truths: The Iroquois' fight for the Olympics" data-vars-index="19" data-vars-link-text="Hard Truths: The Iroquois' fight for the Olympics" data-vars-sub-category="headshot" href="https://www.axios.com/authors/newsdesk/" title="Axios">
           <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
            <amp-img alt="Axios" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-testid="amp-tag" height="40" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://static.axios.com/img/axios-icon.png" width="40">

         <div class="truncate">
          <div class="truncate">
           <a class="text-soft-black-core no-underline hover:text-accent-blue-shade hover:underline gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/authors/newsdesk/" data-vars-content-id="05318243-dc9d-4334-a041-42403824eafe" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Hard Truths: The Iroquois' fight for the Olympics" data-vars-index="19" data-vars-link-text="Hard Truths: The Iroquois' fight for the Olympics" data-vars-sub-category="author-line" href="https://www.axios.com/authors/newsdesk/">
            Axios
           </a>
          </div>
          <span class="mb-12 text-soft-black-shade time-rubric text-tag" data-testid="time-rubric">
           Mar 20, 2021 -
           <a class="text-soft-black-shade no-underline hover:text-accent-blue-shade hover:underline gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="/podcasts" data-vars-content-id="05318243-dc9d-4334-a041-42403824eafe" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Hard Truths: The Iroquois' fight for the Olympics" data-vars-index="19" data-vars-item="timestamp-section-button" data-vars-link-text="Podcasts" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="/podcasts">
            Podcasts
           </a>
          </span>

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/axios-today-podcast-hard-truths-iroquois-lacrosse-olympics-05318243-dc9d-4334-a041-42403824eafe.html" data-vars-content-id="05318243-dc9d-4334-a041-42403824eafe" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Hard Truths: The Iroquois' fight for the Olympics" data-vars-index="19" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="Hard Truths: The Iroquois' fight for the Olympics" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/axios-today-podcast-hard-truths-iroquois-lacrosse-olympics-05318243-dc9d-4334-a041-42403824eafe.html">
          Hard Truths: The Iroquois' fight for the Olympics
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <div class="cbbc7v-0 iNrCiz col-1-13 sm:col-3-11">
          <div>
           <div>
            <amp-megaphone class="i-amphtml-layout-fixed-height i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-episode="AXIOS9856087240" data-light="" height="150" i-amphtml-layout="fixed-height" layout="fixed-height" style="height:150px;">
            </amp-megaphone>
            <div style="display:none">
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </figure>
        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          The latest episode of our Hard Truths series examining systemic racism in America takes a look at the game of lacrosse.
         </p>
         <p>
          It was played by Native Americans as far back as the 12th century. The Iroquois people called it a medicine game — it was spiritual. But this isn’t the predominant image of lacrosse today.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Guest:
          </strong>
          Lyle Thompson, lacrosse player for the Iroquois Nationals.
         </p>
         <p>

           Credits:
          </strong>

           podcasts@axios.com
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </div>

         </a>
        </h3>

            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>

         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           A family of Central American asylum seekers arrives to a bus station after being dropped off by Border Patrol. Photo: John Moore/Getty Images
          </p>

        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          The Biden administration has awarded an $86 million contract for hotel rooms near the border to hold around 1,200 migrant family members who cross the U.S.-Mexico border, DHS officials confirmed to Axios.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Why it matters:
          </strong>
          It's a sign of growing numbers of migrant families trying to come to the U.S. — in addition to already overwhelming numbers of kids crossing the border without their parents or legal guardians. Both trends appear to be straining government resources.
         </p>

        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/degrowth-economic-growth-climate-change-pandemic-774933af-9209-4b74-89fb-b4a783a87305.html" data-vars-content-id="774933af-9209-4b74-89fb-b4a783a87305" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="How stalling growth hurts the planet" data-vars-index="21" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="How stalling growth hurts the planet" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/degrowth-economic-growth-climate-change-pandemic-774933af-9209-4b74-89fb-b4a783a87305.html">
          How stalling growth hurts the planet
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/degrowth-economic-growth-climate-change-pandemic-774933af-9209-4b74-89fb-b4a783a87305.html" data-vars-content-id="774933af-9209-4b74-89fb-b4a783a87305" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="How stalling growth hurts the planet" data-vars-index="21" data-vars-item="featured_image" data-vars-link-text="How stalling growth hurts the planet" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/degrowth-economic-growth-climate-change-pandemic-774933af-9209-4b74-89fb-b4a783a87305.html" title="How stalling growth hurts the planet">
          <div class="dm9ls1-0 bIqTEE">
           <amp-img alt="How stalling growth hurts the planet" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-format="default" data-testid="amp-tag" height="1080" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/6IUALMbWB8ZMIaQXmhJePJOG4fs=/0x0:1920x1080/1920x1080/2021/03/19/1616158335781.jpg" srcset="https://images.axios.com/6IUALMbWB8ZMIaQXmhJePJOG4fs=/0x0:1920x1080/1920x1080/2021/03/19/1616158335781.jpg 1920w,https://images.axios.com/YZh1_Wr8KJwS5WE5Z9xPabb_Mwc=/0x0:1920x1080/1600x900/2021/03/19/1616158335781.jpg 1600w,https://images.axios.com/2aYR6LGmPAsyLG4q5YfeZ6xfpAw=/0x0:1920x1080/1366x768/2021/03/19/1616158335781.jpg 1366w,https://images.axios.com/49WKRCUe5PX2ayPZ4vsWxuDMmME=/0x0:1920x1080/1024x576/2021/03/19/1616158335781.jpg 1024w,https://images.axios.com/-DToUvV8aafb0WDAnSn4Hi-bIFE=/0x0:1920x1080/768x432/2021/03/19/1616158335781.jpg 768w,https://images.axios.com/jY4qOi-yNlqxg6CcqmQlfgtrfeE=/0x0:1920x1080/640x360/2021/03/19/1616158335781.jpg 640w,https://images.axios.com/sN_JehCP_rASmGH5X5pYYO7frgs=/0x0:1920x1080/320x180/2021/03/19/1616158335781.jpg 320w" width="1920">
            <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:56.2500%;">
            </i-amphtml-sizer>
           </amp-img>
          </div>
         </a>
         <figcaption class="sc-31t5q3-8 sc-1jy24uc-1 DCNMo mt-4 sm:mt-6 text-soft-black-shade">
          <p>
           Illustration: Aïda Amer/Axios
          </p>
         </figcaption>
        </figure>
        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          Some environmentalists and economists are pushing for "degrowth" — stabilizing or even shrinking the economy — to avert environmental catastrophe.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           The big picture:
          </strong>
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.degrowth.info/en/what-is-degrowth/" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="16" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="Degrowthism" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.degrowth.info/en/what-is-degrowth/" target="_blank">
           Degrowthism
          </a>
          may seem like the only reasonable response to the climate challenges we face, but the experience of enforced economic shrinking during the pandemic indicates the pain would outweigh the benefits — especially for the world's poorest.
         </p>
        </div>

        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          The handful of gubernatorial contests and special elections throughout 2021 could be the first litmus test of post-Trump politics during the Biden era.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           The state of play:
          </strong>
          2021's slate of contests begins this weekend. Two special elections take place on Saturday in Louisiana. The elections are to replace Rep.-elect Luke Letlow (R), who passed away last year due to COVID-19, and Rep. Cedric Richmond (D), who joined the administration as a Biden senior adviser.
         </p>

      <div class="sc-1jy24uc-0 ehZYCh full gtm-content-click pt-20 up-to-sm:pt-12" data-testid="au-container">
       <div class="sc-1jy24uc-3 jFfnFy grid-layout">
        <div class="flex items-center caption mb-12">
         <div class="w-20 h-20 mr-6 sc-6usfji-0 lbJFqa">
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/authors/dnather/" data-vars-content-id="3142a41a-c771-4f4b-beb7-2cb512d75c19" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Axios-Ipsos poll: The growing sports divide over race and politics" data-vars-index="24" data-vars-link-text="Axios-Ipsos poll: The growing sports divide over race and politics" data-vars-sub-category="headshot" href="https://www.axios.com/authors/dnather/" title="David Nather">

            <amp-img alt="David Nather" class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" data-testid="amp-tag" height="40" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" src="https://images.axios.com/0f0EuS3nDvmcB08tSwNSP9FzIrw=/0x0:328x328/52x0/2020/05/01/1588371058095.jpg" width="40">

          <div class="truncate">
           <a class="text-soft-black-core no-underline hover:text-accent-blue-shade hover:underline gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/authors/dnather/" data-vars-content-id="3142a41a-c771-4f4b-beb7-2cb512d75c19" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Axios-Ipsos poll: The growing sports divide over race and politics" data-vars-index="24" data-vars-link-text="Axios-Ipsos poll: The growing sports divide over race and politics" data-vars-sub-category="author-line" href="https://www.axios.com/authors/dnather/">
            David Nather
           </a>
          </div>
          <span class="mb-12 text-soft-black-shade time-rubric text-tag" data-testid="time-rubric">
           Mar 20, 2021 -
           <a class="text-soft-black-shade no-underline hover:text-accent-blue-shade hover:underline gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="/sports" data-vars-content-id="3142a41a-c771-4f4b-beb7-2cb512d75c19" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Axios-Ipsos poll: The growing sports divide over race and politics" data-vars-index="24" data-vars-item="timestamp-section-button" data-vars-link-text="Sports" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="/sports">
            Sports
           </a>
          </span>
         </div>
        </div>
        <h3 class="font-regular leading-tight mt-0 md:text-h5 lg:text-h4 col-1-13 mb-12 text-h6">
         <a class="title-link gtm-content-click" data-cy="top-story-header-link" data-vars-click-url="https://www.axios.com/axios-ipsos-poll-sports-race-politics-3142a41a-c771-4f4b-beb7-2cb512d75c19.html" data-vars-content-id="3142a41a-c771-4f4b-beb7-2cb512d75c19" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-headline="Axios-Ipsos poll: The growing sports divide over race and politics" data-vars-index="24" data-vars-item="headline" data-vars-link-text="Axios-Ipsos poll: The growing sports divide over race and politics" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit_full" href="https://www.axios.com/axios-ipsos-poll-sports-race-politics-3142a41a-c771-4f4b-beb7-2cb512d75c19.html">
          Axios-Ipsos poll: The growing sports divide over race and politics
         </a>
        </h3>
        <figure class="flex flex-col m-0 mb-8 sm:mb-12 w-full col-1-13" data-testid="au-image">
         <div class="cbbc7v-0 iNrCiz col-1-13 sm:col-3-11">
          <div>
           <div>
            <figure>
             <amp-iframe class="i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" frameborder="0" height="1018" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" resizable="resizable" sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox" src="https://datawrapper.dwcdn.net/ud3Tk/1/" title="" width="1200">
              <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:84.8333%;">
              </i-amphtml-sizer>
              <div aria-label="Expand chart" class="expand-chart" overflow="true" role="button" tabindex="0">
               Expand chart
              </div>
              <amp-img alt="" class="contain i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" height="1018" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" media="(min-width: 769px)" placeholder="true" src="https://datawrapper.dwcdn.net/ud3Tk/fallback.png" width="1200">
               <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:84.8333%;">
               </i-amphtml-sizer>
              </amp-img>
              <amp-img alt="" class="contain i-amphtml-layout-responsive i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" height="1022" i-amphtml-layout="responsive" layout="responsive" media="(max-width: 768px)" placeholder="true" src="https://datawrapper.dwcdn.net/ud3Tk/apple.png" width="750">
               <i-amphtml-sizer style="display:block;padding-top:136.2667%;">
               </i-amphtml-sizer>
              </amp-img>
             </amp-iframe>
            </figure>
            <div style="display:none">
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </figure>
        <div class="sc-31t5q3-7 sc-1jy24uc-2 bUgOWv up-to-sm:mb-4" data-testid="au-axiom">
         <p>
          Americans are divided by race and politics over the appropriateness of political activism in sports, especially when it comes to athletes taking a knee during the national anthem, according to a new
          <a class="gtm-content-click" data-vars-click-url="https://www.ipsos.com/en-us/news-polls/axios-hard-truth-sports-poll-2021" data-vars-event-category="top_stories" data-vars-index="18" data-vars-item="in_content_link" data-vars-link-text="Axios-Ipsos poll" data-vars-sub-category="atomic_unit" href="https://www.ipsos.com/en-us/news-polls/axios-hard-truth-sports-poll-2021" target="_blank">
           Axios-Ipsos poll
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Yes, but:
          </strong>
          The poll also found that Americans have more mixed feelings on the use of Native American-themed mascots, which generate strong opposition among Black Americans while other groups are more open to it.
         </p>
        </div>
